class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364950'>维长安二年岁次月日。司礼主簿宋某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364950_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。敬祭于故宫尹丞太原王君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364950_comment'></div>惟灵显考。抗志恬漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364950_comment'></div>九辟奚顾。一邱自乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364950_comment'></div>行拟巢由。言重许郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364950_comment'></div>粤我先人。比德同道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364950_comment'></div>理阃探索。词源论讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364950_comment'></div>翰墨具存。有真有草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364950_comment'></div>古人之言。朋友世亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364950_comment'></div>王氏兄弟。既义且仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364950_comment'></div>抚我则厚。莫殊天伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364950_comment'></div>粤我幼蒙。哀缠岵屺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364950_comment'></div>急难相顾。若出诸已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364950_comment'></div>闻过必箴。见善斯喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364950_comment'></div>盛德之后。昔闻其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364950_comment'></div>之子壮年。朱绂始光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364950_comment'></div>贺者在门。哭者在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364950_comment'></div>慰君之兄。抚君之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364950_comment'></div>郭门祖祭。平生已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364950_comment'></div>问天何言。闭恨泉里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364950_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364950_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1364950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年</a>　由司礼主簿迁尚方监丞（少府监丞）<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年11月</a>　十一月五日，苏颋为合宫县令，宋有诗相送。作品：送合宫苏明府颋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（苏颋（670-727），字廷硕，京兆武功人，苏瑰（瑰）子。年十七进士及第，神龙中累官至中书舍人，开元四年迁紫微侍郎、知政事、袭封许国公。文思敏捷，与张说并称“燕许大手笔”，开元十五年卒，年五十八，文集三十卷，已佚。《旧唐书》卷八八、《新唐书》卷一二五有传。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第245页苏颋条。）</span><div id='poem_sentence_0_22199'>铉府诞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22199", 22199, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>英规</span>，公才天下知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22199'>谓乘羔雁族，继入凤皇池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22199'>赤县求人隐，青门起路岐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22199'>翟回车少别，凫化舄遥驰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　太平公主子病愈，设斋礼佛，宋为作叹佛文。作品：为太平公主五郎病愈设斋叹佛文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（据文中中宗、韦后尊号及太平公主封号，文作于神龙二年七月至三年八月间，姑系二年。）</span><div id='poem_1364949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为太平公主五郎病愈设斋叹佛文</a><span class='authorDate'>（706年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364949")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364949'>至矣哉。释迦之本愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364949_comment'></div>念起于大悲。业成于广济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364949_comment'></div>代俗以积迷为用。有感斯通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364949_comment'></div>众生以诸病作身。至诚能愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364949_comment'></div>我镇国太平公主。娥灵袭彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364949_comment'></div>女曜联英。戒环佩于中闺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364949_comment'></div>邑山河于外馆。位弥高而迹弥下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364949_comment'></div>保是洪猷。身日贵而心日微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364949_comment'></div>由乎夙植。全其忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364949_comment'></div>颂美于家邦。宜尔子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364949_comment'></div>理归于福寿。第五子某官某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364949_comment'></div>才光性与。慧发生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364949_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364949", 1364949, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>山桂</span>含芳而逼人。阶兰吐秀而惊俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364949_comment'></div>顷以寒暄稍改。保摄微乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364949_comment'></div>留卧玳瑁之床。陪侍凤凰之宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364949_comment'></div>公主上祈妙福。蒙降慈恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364949_comment'></div>汉赐黄金。还依膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364949_comment'></div>隋珍明月。再入掌中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364949_comment'></div>今者上报慈恩。大张名供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364949_comment'></div>于是披甲第。辟梵筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364949_comment'></div>幢盖乘空而下来。龙象接武而爰集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364949_comment'></div>回供纯陁之国。求馔香积之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364949_comment'></div>面为邱而蔽庭。酪为沼而环砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364949_comment'></div>龙王献水。喷车马之埃尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364949_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364949", 1364949, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>天女散花</span>。缀山林之草树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364949_comment'></div>无边之施。下饱于三涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364949_comment'></div>普救之心。傍宽于六趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364949_comment'></div>伏愿以斯妙福。上荐圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364949_comment'></div>应天皇帝长保金图。永临璿极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364949_comment'></div>九族既睦。袪其有漏之缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364949_comment'></div>万人以安。不舍无生之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364949_comment'></div>顺天皇后庆垂椒掖。德盛兰宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364949_comment'></div>国风<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364949", 1364949, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>流洽</span>于鹊巢。坤仪光赞于龙扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364949_comment'></div>皇太子业跻圣敬。本固元良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364949_comment'></div>诸王公主等擢秀本枝。崇荣汤沐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364949_comment'></div>三槐九。庶职群寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364949_comment'></div>咸维赤县之图。共翼青云之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364949_comment'></div>备该空有。遍烛幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364949_comment'></div>俱超解脱之津。永拔轮回之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364949_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1364949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　河北大旱，遣侍御使姚绍之等发吴大仓赈之，宋有诗送姚出使江东。作品：送姚侍御出使江东。<span class='inlineComment2'>（姚绍之，湖州武康人。初以鸾台典仪累迁监察御史。神龙二年，王同皎、张仲之等谋杀武三思，事觉被捕，诏绍之与左台大夫李承嘉按治。绍之酷虐曲成其罪，以功擢左台侍御史，自此意岸轩傲，朝野侧目。与侍御使周利用、冉祖雍、太仆丞李悛、光禄丞宋之逊等五人，为三思耳目，时人呼为“三思五狗”。后坐赃当死，韦后女弟救请，贬岭南琼山尉。俄逃还京，万年尉捕击，折其足。更授南陵令，员外置。开元十三年，为括州长史同正，不得与州事，死。《旧唐书》卷第一八六下、《新唐书》卷二○九有传。《旧唐书·武三思传》：“侍御使周利用、冉祖雍、太仆丞李悛、光禄丞宋之逊、监察御使姚绍之等五人，常为其耳目，时人呼为‘三思五狗’”）</span><div id='poem_allusion_22141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22141'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22141'>帝忧河朔郡，南发海陵仓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22141'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9983, "poem_sentence_2_22141")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_22141", 22141, id='poem_sentence_3_22141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22141'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22141_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年2月</a>　神龙三年二月，帝幸安乐公主宅，宋侍宴应制。作品：宴安乐公主宅。<div id='poem_22201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宴安乐公主宅得空字</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22201")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22201_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22201'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(720, "poem_allusion_22201")'>鲁壁</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1565, "poem_allusion_22201")'>箫奏秦台</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22201'>英藩筑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22201", 22201, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>外馆</span>，爱主出王宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22201'>宾至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22201", 22201, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>星槎</span>落，仙来月宇空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22201'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_22201", 22201, onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1565, "poem_sentence_3_22201")'>箫奏秦台</span>里，书开<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(720, "poem_sentence_3_22201")'>鲁壁</span>中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22201'>短歌能驻日，艳舞欲娇风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22201'>闻有淹留处，山阿满桂丛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22201'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年春</a>　过中书舍人元希声山庄，有诗。作品：过中书元舍人山斋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（元希声（662-707），河南洛阳人，举进士，授内黄主簿，累迁司礼博士，圣历中，预修《三教珠英》，书成以功迁太子文学。历主客、考功员外郎，中宗复位，擢中书舍人，转太常少卿，景龙元年卒吏部侍郎任，年四十六，有文集三十卷。事见崔湜《故吏部侍郎元公碑》、《元和姓纂》卷四、《唐会要》卷三六、卷七五。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第62页元希声条。）</span><div id='poem_825699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_825699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/825699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过中书元舍人山斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_825699")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_825699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_825699'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_825699'>元侯松子宾，寓此掖垣职。<div id='poem_sentence_0_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_825699'>移疾多暇豫，孤斋恣閒息。<div id='poem_sentence_1_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_825699'>修径接大野，重峦跨南北。<div id='poem_sentence_2_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_825699'>具物芬荣时，登攀各可极。<div id='poem_sentence_3_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_825699'>林间百鸟变，郊外千花织。<div id='poem_sentence_4_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_825699'>秦岭似云横，周原如黛饰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_825699'>洛中昔游衍，常闻故园忆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_825699'>清言尽场圃，嘉话数耘植。<div id='poem_sentence_7_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_825699'>梦想恒载驰，松篁若旧识。<div id='poem_sentence_8_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_825699'>酒情忽无限，琴意忻有得。<div id='poem_sentence_9_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_825699'>更阅青溪诗，逾励丹霞食。<div id='poem_sentence_10_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_825699'>贵者日已远，幸君惠容色。<div id='poem_sentence_11_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_825699'>朅来休颍阳，任予孤且直<span class='inlineComment2'>（同前见《大典》卷二五三九。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_825699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_825699'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_825699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年春</a>　游宴兵部韦员外韦曲庄，宋赋诗并序。作品：春游宴兵部韦员外韦曲庄序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（韦员外：中宗韦后族人，名未详。宋之问等所赋四韵诗已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1364942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春游宴兵部韦员外韦曲庄序</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364942")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364942'>长安城南有韦曲庄。京郊之形胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364942_comment'></div>却倚城阙。朱雀起而为门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364942_comment'></div>斜枕冈峦。黑龙卧而周宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364942_comment'></div>贤臣作相。旧号儒宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364942_comment'></div>圣后配元。今为戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364942_comment'></div>韦大官双珠绝价。百金懿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364942_comment'></div>文华得俊于陆氏。兄弟掩誉于荀家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364942_comment'></div>先人结庐。当大厦之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364942_comment'></div>众宾连袂。乘暮春之月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364942_comment'></div>观其奥区一曲。甲第千甍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364942_comment'></div>冠盖列东西之居。公侯开南北之巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364942_comment'></div>嬴女楼下。吹凤降于神仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364942_comment'></div>汉妃馆前。濯龙走其车马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364942_comment'></div>地灵磊落而閒出。天爵蝉联而相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364942_comment'></div>拜郎起草。袭雁而传羔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364942_comment'></div>补衮司槐。送伯而迎季。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364942_comment'></div>尔乃辟虚幌。敞华筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364942_comment'></div>闺门之秀士咸集。京邑之清流毕萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364942_comment'></div>万株果树。色杂云霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364942_comment'></div>千亩竹林。气含烟雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364942_comment'></div>激樊川而萦碧濑。浸以成陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364942_comment'></div>望太乙而邻少微。森然逼座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364942_comment'></div>尚书未至。曳履惊邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364942_comment'></div>宫尹递来。鸣驺动壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364942_comment'></div>登玉俎。醉金觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364942_comment'></div>地高而珍物虽丰。理洞而清徽不杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364942_comment'></div>以醉观德。因谈获情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364942_comment'></div>外戚遨游。自携歌吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364942_comment'></div>主人赏会。但有琴诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364942_comment'></div>于是下高台。陟曲沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364942_comment'></div>铺落花以为茵。结垂杨而代幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364942_comment'></div>霁景含日。晚霞五彩而丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364942_comment'></div>韶望卷云。春膏一色而凝黛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364942_comment'></div>景阑兴逸。气清心远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364942_comment'></div>仰大儒之肆。其德可师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364942_comment'></div>入处士之庐。斯人若在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364942_comment'></div>讽诵于逸彭之藻。沐浴于扶阳之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364942_comment'></div>向来挹清议。擅风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364942_comment'></div>即事奇伟。佳辰行乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364942_comment'></div>安可无述。文在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364942_comment'></div>酆国善诱词宗。见收士末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364942_comment'></div>内史褉亭之集。窃倚琳琅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364942_comment'></div>卫尉别业之游。滥先题目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364942_comment'></div>归轩莫驻。丽城将掩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364942_comment'></div>拙而不速。恨无倚马之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364942_comment'></div>婉而且微。请谈雕龙之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364942_comment'></div>公命赋水字。盍成四韵云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364942_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1364942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年7月</a>　武三思为太子重俊起兵所杀，追封梁王，宋代三思妃为让封表。作品：为梁王武三思妃让封表。<div id='poem_1364928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为梁王武三思妃让封表</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364928")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364928'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364928'>妾言。妾闻天与才多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364928_comment'></div>地居外戚。理乖谦益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364928_comment'></div>患在宠盈。妾亡夫三思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364928_comment'></div>颇读圣贤之书。夙知止足之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364928_comment'></div>在先朝锡汉藩之社。位亚上台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364928_comment'></div>陛下流渭阳之思。室嫔爱主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364928_comment'></div>常恐官高禄厚。福极祸来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364928_comment'></div>闺门之谈。颠覆存戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364928_comment'></div>但以愿施尘露之效。尚郁山林之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364928_comment'></div>讵谓吴楚指有宠为名。父子以无辜同枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364928_comment'></div>良以崇高取忌。退让未形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364928_comment'></div>事虽噬脐。言犹在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364928_comment'></div>妾夫埋黄壤。子夭青春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364928_comment'></div>唯知哀诉神明。号泣天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364928_comment'></div>妾之残命。称曰未亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364928_comment'></div>更何心颜。享兹丰厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364928_comment'></div>况三思久谋谦退。人所未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364928_comment'></div>实恐士庶游谈。是非相半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364928_comment'></div>既未能辨明高义。岂复忍贪吝馀资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364928_comment'></div>虽则伯宗已亡。献诫者闻乎奸盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364928_comment'></div>尚冀黔娄宿意。见知者因乎寡妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364928_comment'></div>今坟土未乾。繐帷犹设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364928_comment'></div>妾所以废寝忘飧。沥款披诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364928_comment'></div>未允前祈。更陈后请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364928_comment'></div>伏愿俯矜贱妾。远念幽魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364928_comment'></div>收彼白茅之封。表其赤松之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364928_comment'></div>光陛下有任贤之德。明三思无冒宠之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364928_comment'></div>妾之区区。意尽于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364928_comment'></div>无任感切之至。谨遣某诣朝堂上表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364928_comment'></div>再黩威严。伏深战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364928_comment'></div>妾死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364928_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1364928_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年冬</a>　神龙三年七月兵变，武三思父子死，冬，宋有挽词悼武三思。作品：梁宣王挽词三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（武三思（-707），并州文水人，武则天之侄。少以武后族累转右卫将军，则天临朝，擢拜夏官尚书。天授元年，拜天官尚书。证圣元年，转春官尚书、监修国史。契丹陷营州，为榆关道安抚大使屯兵。神功元年，同凤阁鸾台三品。圣历中，一拜内史，罢为特进、太子少保。后迁太子宾客，仍监修国史。神龙初，进拜司空、同中书门下三品，固辞不受，未几，随例降封为德静郡王，寻拜左散骑常侍。与安乐公主密谋废太子，神龙三年七月为太子率羽林军所杀。三思略通文史，曾预修《三教珠英》、《则天皇后实录》。生平事迹见《旧唐书》卷一八三、《新唐书》卷二○六本传、《唐会要》卷六三、《资治通鉴》卷二○六、卷二○八等。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第477页武三思条。）</span><div class='authorDate'>（707年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22156")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22156_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22156'><span "poem_allusion_22156")'>尧母</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22156_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22156'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22156'>贵藩<span "poem_sentence_3_22156")'>置醴</span>人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_22157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22157'>可叹虞歌夕，纷纷骑吹回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年冬</a>　神龙三年七月兵变，武三思父子死，冬，宋有挽词悼武崇训。作品：鲁忠王挽词三首。<div id='poem_22165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_22167'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年11月4日</a>　宰相宗楚客兄弟祭梁王武三思，宋为作祭文。作品：为宗尚书祭梁宣王文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宗尚书：宗楚客（-710），字叔敖，蒲州河东人，则天从姊子。武后朝，官至宰相。神龙中，附韦后及武三思，三思引为兵部尚书、同中书门下三品，韦后败，伏诛。《旧唐书》卷九二、《新唐书》卷一○九有传。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第536页宗楚客条。将作大匠：宗晋卿（-710），宰相宗楚客弟，武后朝，以奸赃事发，兄弟配流岭外，秦客死，晋卿等寻复追还，附韦后及武三思，神龙中，累迁将作大匠。韦氏败，亦被诛。附见《旧唐书》卷九二、《新唐书》卷一○九《宗楚客传》，参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第536页宗晋卿条。）</span><div id='poem_1364953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为宗尚书祭梁宣王文</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年11月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364953")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364953'>维大唐景龙元年岁次丁未十月乙未朔四月戊戌。兵部尚书宗楚客弟将作大匠秦客等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364953_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。致祭于梁宣王之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364953_comment'></div>惟王神岳降灵。英姿济代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364953_comment'></div>在周锡梁社之宠。翊唐有代邸之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364953_comment'></div>不谓业在必安。而衅生非意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364953_comment'></div>贼臣结党。大黩宸闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364953_comment'></div>逆子弄兵。轻诬懿戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364953_comment'></div>密谋奉主。惟以国家为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364953_comment'></div>飞祸及门。翻令父子并命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364953_comment'></div>九重轸念。悼舟楫之堙没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364953_comment'></div>百辟兴嗟。怆衣冠之殄瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364953_comment'></div>楚客等早承辉眄。夙忝娱游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364953_comment'></div>姻属谬接于葭莩。兄弟窃方于雁序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364953_comment'></div>叨列五等。同事两朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364953_comment'></div>昔以高义铭心。今犹德音在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364953_comment'></div>严慈永往。伯季凋零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364953_comment'></div>友睦申于长妹。成立冀于犹子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364953_comment'></div>而家不悔祸。俱毙仇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364953_comment'></div>入私庭而痛深。过王门而悲极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364953_comment'></div>竹池旧赏。看雁鹜之犹归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364953_comment'></div>蒿里新歌。恨天人之永逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364953_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。九原撰日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364953_comment'></div>万古营魂。士悲高驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364953_comment'></div>帝恸津门。殒贤辅而星坼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364953_comment'></div>害良臣而雾昏。想平生之如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364953_comment'></div>庶髣髴于斯樽。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364953_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1364953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年10月</a>　七月太子重俊政变，帝后登玄武门得免。八月改玄武门为神武门，十月韦后上《神武颂》，宋为百官请造颂碑表。作品：为文武百寮等请造神武颂碑表。<div id='poem_1364933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为文武百寮等请造神武颂碑表</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364933")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364933'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364933'>臣某等闻行至公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364933_comment'></div>莫先于发挥茂实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364933_comment'></div>垂不朽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364933_comment'></div>不若于刊纪鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364933_comment'></div>伏惟应天神圣皇帝陛下一德披图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364933_comment'></div>五精乘运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364933_comment'></div>先天地而利用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364933_comment'></div>依鬼神以制法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364933_comment'></div>无思不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364933_comment'></div>有感必通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364933_comment'></div>日者变起心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364933_comment'></div>祸生肘腋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364933_comment'></div>弄兵指阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364933_comment'></div>敢忘下济之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364933_comment'></div>犯门斩关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364933_comment'></div>遂激上灵之愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364933_comment'></div>陛下近幸元武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364933_comment'></div>傍顾紫微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364933_comment'></div>凤翔而枭獍失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364933_comment'></div>龙见而鲸鲵就戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364933_comment'></div>顺天翊圣皇后配乾积德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364933_comment'></div>从帝居尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364933_comment'></div>佐莫大之英猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364933_comment'></div>参非常之妙略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364933_comment'></div>亲纡宝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364933_comment'></div>式颂元猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364933_comment'></div>椒掖之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364933_comment'></div>久垂河汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364933_comment'></div>甘泉之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364933_comment'></div>已入京都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364933_comment'></div>伏惟陛下卑奉圣躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364933_comment'></div>谦保神器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364933_comment'></div>惜其国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364933_comment'></div>念彼人艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364933_comment'></div>有命且停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364933_comment'></div>含灵失望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364933_comment'></div>臣等容光寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364933_comment'></div>窃位明朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364933_comment'></div>不蚕而衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364933_comment'></div>无裨尘露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364933_comment'></div>不耕而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364933_comment'></div>有负灵祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364933_comment'></div>陛下寝有道之丰碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364933_comment'></div>臣等享无功之厚载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364933_comment'></div>亭育虽广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364933_comment'></div>何所自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364933_comment'></div>且天惠不可以阙书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364933_comment'></div>神功不可以久寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364933_comment'></div>臣等请各减所俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364933_comment'></div>以勒殊休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364933_comment'></div>庶同子来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364933_comment'></div>成之匪日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364933_comment'></div>无任光开垂裕之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1364933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_22129'>柳河悽挽曲，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9310, "poem_sentence_2_22129")'>薤露</span>湿灵衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22129'>一厝穷泉闭，双鸾遂不飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22129'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年</a>　长安令马搆乞让己封阶以封亡母，宋为之状。作品：为长安马明府亡母请邑号状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（马明府：马搆，据张说《故洛阳尉赠朝散大夫马府君碑》，知马搆曾官太子仆，景龙初为长安令。上书乞让己赐阶以封亡母，时人谓之孝。余不详。）</span><div id='poem_1364934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年</a>　迁官户部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年5月5日</a>　入修文馆为学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年秋</a>　宰相宗楚客兄弟祭鲁忠王武崇训，宋为作祭文。作品：为宗尚书兄弟祭鲁忠王文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宗尚书：宗楚客（-710），字叔敖，蒲州河东人，则天从姊子。武后朝，官至宰相。神龙中，附韦后及武三思，三思引为兵部尚书、同中书门下三品，韦后败，伏诛。《旧唐书》卷九二、《新唐书》卷一○九有传。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第536页宗楚客条。将作大匠：宗晋卿（-710），宰相宗楚客弟，武后朝，以奸赃事发，兄弟配流岭外，秦客死，晋卿等寻复追还，附韦后及武三思，神龙中，累迁将作大匠。韦氏败，亦被诛。附见《旧唐书》卷九二、《新唐书》卷一○九《宗楚客传》，参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第536页宗晋卿条。）</span><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年秋</a>　弟宋之悌赴许州司马任，宋有诗相送。作品：送许州宋司马之任。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：陶注云宋司马当是宋之问弟之逊或之悌。宋之逊以神龙二年告变之功授光禄丞，且为武三思亲信党羽，其势未衰，且兄宋之问亦以倾附武、韦正得势，之逊似不会有外迁司马之事；且当时有李适等一批景龙文馆学士相送之盛，也不似左迁。故疑当时外任司马之人或为资历稍浅之宋之悌，非之逊。）</span><div id='poem_22137' id='poem_sentence_6_22189_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年10月</a>　十月国子主簿杜审言卒，东葬缑氏山，宋作祭文遥祭。作品：祭杜学士审言文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（杜审言：字必简，祖籍襄阳，迁居巩县。咸亨元年登进士第，授隰城尉，累转洛阳丞。圣历元年，贬吉州司户参军，被构下狱，免官还洛阳。授著作郎，俄迁膳部员外郎。神龙元年，因阿附张易之，流峰州。二年召还，授国子监主簿，加修文馆直学士。景龙二年卒，年六十余。少与李峤、崔融、苏味道齐名，号文章四友。有文集十卷。《旧唐书》卷一九○上、《新唐书》卷二○一有传。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第255页杜审言条。）</span><div id='poem_1364956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭社学士审言文</a><span class='authorDate'>（708年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364956")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364956'>维大唐景龙二年岁次戊申月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364956_comment'></div>考功员外郎宋之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364956_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364956_comment'></div>敬祭于故修文馆学士杜君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364956_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364956_comment'></div>位曰大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364956_comment'></div>才曰天爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364956_comment'></div>辞业备而官成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364956_comment'></div>名声高而命薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364956_comment'></div>屈原不终于楚相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364956_comment'></div>扬雄自投于汉阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364956_comment'></div>代生人而岂无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364956_comment'></div>人违代而咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364956_comment'></div>运钟唐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364956_comment'></div>崇文宠儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364956_comment'></div>国求至宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364956_comment'></div>家献灵珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364956_comment'></div>后复有王杨卢骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364956_comment'></div>继之以子跃云衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364956_comment'></div>王也才参卿于西陕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364956_comment'></div>杨也终远宰于东吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364956_comment'></div>卢则哀其栖山而卧疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364956_comment'></div>骆则不能保族而全躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364956_comment'></div>由运然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364956_comment'></div>莫以福寿自卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364956_comment'></div>将神忌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364956_comment'></div>不得华实斯俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364956_comment'></div>惟灵昭昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364956_comment'></div>度越诸子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364956_comment'></div>言必得俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364956_comment'></div>意常通理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364956_comment'></div>其含润也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364956_comment'></div>若和风欲曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364956_comment'></div>摇露气于春林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364956_comment'></div>其秉艳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364956_comment'></div>似凉雨半晴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364956_comment'></div>悬日光于秋水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364956_comment'></div>众辙同遵者摈落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364956_comment'></div>群心不际者探拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364956_comment'></div>人也不幸而则亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364956_comment'></div>名兮可大而不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364956_comment'></div>君之栖遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364956_comment'></div>自昔迷方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364956_comment'></div>逢时泰兮欲达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364956_comment'></div>闻数奇兮自伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364956_comment'></div>属文母之丕运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364956_comment'></div>应才子之明扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364956_comment'></div>援沦秀于兰畹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364956_comment'></div>侍仙游于柏梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364956_comment'></div>命以著作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364956_comment'></div>拜之为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364956_comment'></div>始翔鸳于清列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364956_comment'></div>旋御魅于炎荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364956_comment'></div>遗旅雁兮超彭蠡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364956_comment'></div>作编人兮居越裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364956_comment'></div>殊许靖之新适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364956_comment'></div>忆虞翻之旧乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364956_comment'></div>惟皇龙兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364956_comment'></div>仰赤墀兮非远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364956_comment'></div>谓白首兮方遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364956_comment'></div>君病何病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364956_comment'></div>到此弥留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364956_comment'></div>药虽饵兮宁愈。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364956_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364956_comment'></div>君之将亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364956_comment'></div>其言也善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364956_comment'></div>余向十旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364956_comment'></div>日或再展。<div id='poem_sentence_107_1364956_comment'></div>相识有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364956_comment'></div>见贤增勖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364956_comment'></div>登君词赋于云台之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364956_comment'></div>将告良友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364956_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_124_1364956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年11月5日</a>　十一月五日帝诞辰，内殿宴群臣，效柏梁体与李适、李峤、上官婉儿等联句，宋预其中。作品：十一月诞辰内殿宴群臣效柏梁体联句。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年11月</a>　汝南王韦洵归葬，宰相韦安石等献祭，宋为作祭文。作品：为韦特进已下祭汝南王文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（韦特进：韦安石（651-714），京兆万年人。举明经，调乾封尉，久视元年，官至文昌右丞、同平章事。神龙元年，迁中书令，封郧国公，加特进。开元元年出为蒲州刺史，转青州刺史，二年贬沔州别驾，愤激而卒，年六十四。《旧唐书》卷九二、《新唐书》卷一二二有传。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第74页韦安石条。）</span><div id='poem_1364955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为韦特进已下祭汝南王文</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364955'>维大唐景龙二年岁次戊申月日。某官某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364955_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。祭于汝南王之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364955_comment'></div>相门踵德。王实挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364955_comment'></div>天资温克。神与聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364955_comment'></div>人称玉树。我嗣金籯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364955_comment'></div>芝庭欲秀。桂林将逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364955_comment'></div>惟彼雁堂。坠兹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364955", 1364955, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>鸿陆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364955_comment'></div>魅夺精气。坟迷草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364955_comment'></div>汉皇纂箓。周母参功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364955_comment'></div>夷夏昭洗。幽明感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364955_comment'></div>九魂见日。一叶随风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364955_comment'></div>孝极先妃。丹旐前归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364955_comment'></div>慈殷诸季。素旐相次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364955_comment'></div>楚氓啜泣。秦人下泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364955_comment'></div>荆分自久。棣落无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364955_comment'></div>悲炎海之下制。惟观津之上书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364955_comment'></div>鸢忌南而跕水。雁爱北而随车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364955_comment'></div>呜呼。凡在枝戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364955_comment'></div>衔恩极遍。宠贲濯龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364955_comment'></div>荣分化燕。独伤元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364955_comment'></div>冥寞无见。玉宸下感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364955_comment'></div>金屋增悲。珠亡祸速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364955_comment'></div>沙崩庆迟。绿车为赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364955_comment'></div>黄泉各思。官舍攸止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364955_comment'></div>先茔甫托。齐国返葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364955_comment'></div>随原可作。灵之归来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364955_comment'></div>无惑瓯骆。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364955_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22194_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年1月</a>　昆明池赋诗，群臣应制百余篇，唯沈宋二诗争胜。作品：奉和晦日幸昆明池应制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《唐诗纪事》卷三“上官昭容”条：“中宗（正月）晦日（农历每月最后一天为晦日）幸昆明池赋诗，群臣应制百余篇，帐殿前结彩楼，命（上官）昭容选一首为新翻御制曲。从臣悉集其下，须臾纸落如飞，各认其名而怀之。既进，唯沈、宋二诗不下。又移时，一纸飞坠，竞取而观，乃沈诗也。及闻其评曰：二诗工力悉敌，沈诗落句云：微臣凋朽质，羞睹豫章材，盖词气已竭。宋诗云：不愁明月尽，自有夜珠来，犹陟健举。沈乃伏，不敢复争。”）</span><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年3月3日</a>　上巳泛舟昆明池，宴宗主簿席，宋赋诗并序。作品：上巳泛舟昆明池宴宗主簿席序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宗主簿：宗邕，据序，当是中书令宗楚客之子。）</span><div id='poem_1364940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上巳泛舟昆明池宴宗主簿席序</a><span class='authorDate'>（709年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364940")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364940'>仆不游于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364940_comment'></div>十有五载矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364940_comment'></div>心由物感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364940_comment'></div>遐矣不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364940_comment'></div>迹为事牵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364940_comment'></div>近而难挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364940_comment'></div>南阳宗邕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364940_comment'></div>文通学古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364940_comment'></div>器重名高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364940_comment'></div>令君有奉倩象贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364940_comment'></div>丞相生元成迈德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364940_comment'></div>暮春修以文之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364940_comment'></div>上巳邀韨褉之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364940_comment'></div>乃结缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364940_comment'></div>撰清辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364940_comment'></div>殷殷辚辚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364940_comment'></div>歊雾惊尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364940_comment'></div>望于昆明之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364940_comment'></div>观其大浸川陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364940_comment'></div>博资畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364940_comment'></div>凫鹥发海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364940_comment'></div>来往沈浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364940_comment'></div>日月丽天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364940_comment'></div>东西出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364940_comment'></div>千年珍馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364940_comment'></div>无复豫章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364940_comment'></div>四面金堤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364940_comment'></div>仍同树杞。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年3月</a>　袁侍御设宴饯永昌丞独孤册赴任，宋赋诗并序。作品：袁侍御席饯永昌独孤少府序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（袁侍御：袁守一，《朝野佥载》卷二：“袁守一任万年尉，于中书令宗楚客门饷生菜，除监察，改右台侍御史。无何，楚客以反诛，守一以其党配流端州。独孤少府：独孤册，字伯谋，河南人，开元中历殿中侍御史，户部郎中，襄州刺史。见《唐郎官石柱题名考》卷一一。宋之问等送独孤册四韵诗，均佚。）</span><div id='poem_1364947' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年夏</a>　与吏部郎中韦抗唱和。作品：敬和吏部韦郎中庭前朱槿之作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（韦抗（667-726），京兆万年人。弱冠明经及第，补魏州参军。累迁殿中侍御史，转主客、吏部二员外郎，进吏部郎中。景云初，为永昌令，迁御史中丞兼礼部尚书。转兵部尚书。开元三年，自太子左庶子出为益州长史。四年，入拜黄门侍郎。历鸿胪卿、御史大夫，出为安州都督。十一年，入拜大理卿，迁刑部尚书，封武阳伯。十四年卒，赠太子太傅。事见《旧唐书》卷九二、《新唐书》卷一二二、苏颋《刑部尚书韦抗神道碑》。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第74页韦抗条。）</span><div class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22083")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_22083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22083'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22083'>粉壁图仙鹤，昂藏真气多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22083'>鶱飞竟不去，当是恋恩波。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22083'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_22083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年秋</a>　与景龙文馆学士分题咏浣纱篇赠陆上人。作品：浣纱篇赠陆上人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗当宋之问景龙二年五月至三年秋为学士时作，姑系三年。陆上人，未详。）</span><div id='poem_22252' id='poem_sentence_0_22252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22252'>国微不自宠，献作吴宫娃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22252'>始觉冶容妄，方悟群<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作君）</span>心邪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作斜）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22252'>钦子秉幽意，世人共<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_22252", 22252, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>称嗟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22252'>愿言托君怀，倘类蓬生麻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22252'>家住雷门曲，高阁凌飞霞。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22252'>淋漓翠羽帐，旖旎采<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年秋</a>　秋晚游普耀寺，有诗。<div id='poem_22134' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22134' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22134?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋晚游普耀寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（709年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22134")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22134_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22134'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22134'>薄暮曲江头，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22134", 22134, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>仁祠</span>暂可留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22134'>山形无隐霁，野色遍呈秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22134'>荷覆香泉密，藤缘宝树幽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22134'>平生厌尘事，过<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作遇）</span>此忽悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22134'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22134_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年</a>　为怀州刺史皇甫知常作让官表。作品：为皇甫怀州让官表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇甫怀州：皇甫知常。《千唐志斋藏志》七○四《大唐故□□门卫长史安定皇甫公（慎）墓志铭》：“父知常，汾、怀、汴等六州刺史，杨、洛二州长史。”皇甫慎开元十九年卒，其父知常与宋之问同时。表约景龙中作。姑系本年。《全唐文》卷八三五重收此表为钱珝文，钱珝为唐末人，当误。）</span><div id='poem_1364926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为皇甫怀州让官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（709年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364926")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364926'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364926'>臣某言。伏奉今月一日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364926_comment'></div>除臣使持节怀州诸军事守怀州刺史。成命俯临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364926_comment'></div>兢魂自失。妨贤不退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364926_comment'></div>无德而升。恩屡锡而知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364926_comment'></div>禄弥高而转惧。中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364926_comment'></div>臣闻国经选士。有一善而不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364926_comment'></div>天爵与能。从九徵而可试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364926_comment'></div>臣薄游宪府。累践礼闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364926_comment'></div>衣绣无执之才。起草愧含香之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364926_comment'></div>移官望苑。日月其除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364926_comment'></div>骖驾梁园。涓埃莫效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364926_comment'></div>剖符南岘。既恧民谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364926_comment'></div>作镇西河。未宽人隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364926_comment'></div>二邦为政。抚熊轼而无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364926_comment'></div>八使回轩。同鹤鸣而有荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364926_comment'></div>遂乃谬沾束帛。猥赐褒扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364926_comment'></div>顿掩前瑕。更延今宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364926_comment'></div>山阳大郡。河内名区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364926_comment'></div>桑竹映淇水之西。井田杂邙山之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364926_comment'></div>将何以润通京邑。化接神州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364926_comment'></div>虽勉三载之勤。何补一年之借。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364926_comment'></div>封畿之要。历选称难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364926_comment'></div>臣也胡颜。敢膺斯寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364926_comment'></div>伏乞再求遗玉。更网潜珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364926_comment'></div>庶使贤才申共理之心。圣主得分忧之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364926_comment'></div>无任叨窃之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈让以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364926_comment'></div>臣所让人。别状封进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364926_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1364926_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年</a>　送怀州刺史皇甫知常赴任，宋赋诗并序。作品：送怀州皇甫使君序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇甫怀州：皇甫知常。《千唐志斋藏志》七○四《大唐故□□门卫长史安定皇甫公（慎）墓志铭》：“父知常，汾、怀、汴等六州刺史，杨、洛二州长史。”皇甫慎开元十九年卒，其父知常与宋之问同时。序景龙元至三年中作，姑系本年。宋之问等送皇甫知常诗，均佚。）</span><div id='poem_1364943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送怀州皇甫使君序</a><span class='authorDate'>（709年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364943")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364943'>甸服三百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364943_comment'></div>共京都参化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364943_comment'></div>良吏二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364943_comment'></div>与天子分忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364943_comment'></div>覃怀奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364943_comment'></div>必寄能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364943_comment'></div>皇甫使君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364943_comment'></div>累司宠职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364943_comment'></div>夙著香名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364943_comment'></div>威惠历刺于外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364943_comment'></div>风流载款于京国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364943_comment'></div>议者应南宫之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364943_comment'></div>实谓光朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364943_comment'></div>使乎奏西河之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364943_comment'></div>更劳为郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364943_comment'></div>襜帷即路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364943_comment'></div>供帐出郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364943_comment'></div>宿雨碧滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364943_comment'></div>浮汉城之气色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364943_comment'></div>朝阳红景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364943_comment'></div>入太山之草树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364943_comment'></div>新丰美酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364943_comment'></div>不换离心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364943_comment'></div>函谷重关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364943_comment'></div>能摇别恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364943_comment'></div>河内未理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364943_comment'></div>暂借寇恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364943_comment'></div>颍川既辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364943_comment'></div>伫归黄霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364943_comment'></div>庙堂侧席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364943_comment'></div>群公以尚义相高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364943_comment'></div>川陆分途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364943_comment'></div>我辈以赠言为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364943_comment'></div>况筵开灞岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364943_comment'></div>路指太行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364943_comment'></div>请居人赠王粲之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364943_comment'></div>去者留阮公之作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1364943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年</a>　送洛州司法参军裴五自长安赴任，宋赋诗并序。作品：送裴五司法赴都序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（裴五：名未详。时裴五当为洛州司法参军，自长安赴任。宋序景龙中作，姑系本年。）</span><div id='poem_1364946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送裴五司法赴都序</a><span class='authorDate'>（709年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364946")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364946'>夫有别必感。今昔共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364946_comment'></div>盖理迫聚散。事均穷达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364946_comment'></div>望秦是断肠之所。况念故园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364946_comment'></div>怀洛多掩涕之人。更分良友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364946_comment'></div>裴五官业传河宝。才诞岳灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364946_comment'></div>彩思有神。须眉若画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364946_comment'></div>一日不见。鄙吝都生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364946_comment'></div>千里送归。风流忽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364946_comment'></div>朝英出饯。回北走于郊隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364946_comment'></div>野墅销雰。引南山于庭际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364946_comment'></div>客饮恨而欢促。席含情而景迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364946_comment'></div>目乔树之将华。青门恋旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364946_comment'></div>背芳萱之稍吐。金谷逢春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364946_comment'></div>举杯伊何。愿君轸之少驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364946_comment'></div>赋诗于是。旌予志之所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364946_comment'></div>敢谓座宾。盍宣离唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364946_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1364946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年秋</a>　中宗将用为中书舍人，太平公主发其知贡举时赇饷狼籍，下迁汴州长史。未行，改越州长史。<br /></div>
-----end

洛阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=684')">679-684年</a>，24-29岁</div><div id='1d41752f361d49e08c6852e39fa2ede4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=682')">679-682年</a>　在洛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　赋太平公主山池。作品：太平公主山池赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陶注云赋称太平未及“镇国”之号，赋当作于高宗后期或武后朝。按：赋云“禀金后之玄训”，称则天为“金后”，知则天尚未称帝。故赋当作于高宗后期或武后天授元年称帝前。姑系高宗之末。太平公主山池在长安还是洛阳，待考。）</span><div id='poem_1364923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太平公主山池赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364923")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364923'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364923'>粤若公主诞生。皇家太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364923_comment'></div>徵郡国以选号。叶时雍之美名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364923_comment'></div>孕灵娥之秀彩。辉婺女之淳精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364923_comment'></div>虹美电熠。兰香玉清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364923_comment'></div>禀金后之元训。系列圣之聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364923_comment'></div>厌绮罗与丝竹。爱瑶池及赤城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364923_comment'></div>搆仙山兮既毕。侔造化之神术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364923_comment'></div>其为状也。攒怪石而岑崟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364923_comment'></div>其为异也。含清气而萧瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364923_comment'></div>列海岸而争耸。分水亭而对出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364923_comment'></div>其东则峰崖刻划。洞穴萦回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364923_comment'></div>乍若风飘雨洒兮移郁岛。又似波沈浪息兮见蓬莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364923_comment'></div>图万重于积石。匿千岭于天台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364923_comment'></div>荆门揭起兮壁峻。少室丛生兮剑开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364923_comment'></div>削成秀绝。莲华之覆高掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364923_comment'></div>独立窈窕。神女之戏阳台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364923_comment'></div>尔其樵溪钓浦。茅堂菌阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364923_comment'></div>秘仙洞之瑶膏。隐山家之场藿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364923_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>烟岑</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/36/Comments/1")'>水涯</span>。缭绕逶迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364923_comment'></div>翠莲瑶草。的烁纷披。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364923_comment'></div>映江浔而烂烂。浮海上而累累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364923_comment'></div>乃之罘与衡霍。岂吾人之所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364923_comment'></div>向背重复。参差反覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364923_comment'></div>翳荟蒙茏。含青吐红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364923_comment'></div>阳崖夺锦。阴壑生风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364923_comment'></div>奇树抱石。新花灌丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364923_comment'></div>向若天长地久兮苔藓合。古往今来兮林涧空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364923_comment'></div>始燕秦而开径。访灵药乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364923_comment'></div>其西则翠屏崭岩。山路诘曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364923_comment'></div>高阁翔云。丹岩吐绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364923_comment'></div>惚兮恍。涉弱水兮至昆崙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364923_comment'></div>杳兮冥。乘龙梁兮向巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364923_comment'></div>壮岷嶓兮连属。郁氛氲兮断续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364923_comment'></div>岩虚兮谷峻。藏清兮蓄韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364923_comment'></div>含珠兮蕴玉。众彩兮明润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364923_comment'></div>芳园暮兮白日沈。爽气浮兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>黛壑</span>深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364923_comment'></div>风泉活活兮鸣石。葛藟青青兮蔓岑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364923_comment'></div>罗八方之奇兽。聚六合之珍禽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364923_comment'></div>别有复道三袭。平台四注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364923_comment'></div>跨渚兮交林。蒸云兮起雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364923_comment'></div>鸳鸯水兮凤凰楼。文虹桥兮彩鹢舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364923_comment'></div>山池成兮帝子游。试一望兮消人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364923_comment'></div>召七贤。集五侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364923_comment'></div>棹浦曲。席岩幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364923_comment'></div>鸣玉佩兮登降。列金觞兮献酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364923_comment'></div>未穷观而极览。忽云散而风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364923_comment'></div>于是乎上客既旋。重扃严闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364923_comment'></div>榜童俨而齐发。䌽女分而为卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364923_comment'></div>牵水叶兮张水嬉。摘山花兮咏山圻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364923_comment'></div>燕姬荆艳兮代所稀。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>凤舞鸾歌</span>兮俨欲飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364923_comment'></div>披烟弄月兮宵未归。桂枝清雾兮湿罗衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364923_comment'></div>奕奕济济。夜旋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>玉邸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364923_comment'></div>隐隐崇崇。朝趋帝宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364923_comment'></div>银炉翕习。烟生雾集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364923_comment'></div>绛节缤纷。扬光吐文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364923_comment'></div>行轩节水。去马腾云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364923_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>锵锵翼翼</span>兮驰丹阙。超超遥遥兮向紫氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364923_comment'></div>宠极兮慈掌。情勤兮幽赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364923_comment'></div>恋宸扆兮出入。忆幽山兮来往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364923_comment'></div>采<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/118/Comments/0")'>朱萼</span>兮山之侧。步兰庭兮候颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364923_comment'></div>掇绿蘋兮于涧潦。宜室家兮叶仇好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364923_comment'></div>既而贞心内洁。淑则远传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364923_comment'></div>诙谈者闻之而必劝。薄者闻之而凛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364923_comment'></div>况复淮王招隐。秦主随仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364923_comment'></div>弄紫房之琴瑟。驰碧落之风烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364923_comment'></div>宾屈宋于珠履。引邻枚于玳筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364923_comment'></div>秋叶飞兮散红树。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>春苔</span>生兮覆绿泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364923_comment'></div>春秋寒暑兮岁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1364923", 1364923, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>荣落</span>。林峦沼沚兮日芳鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364923_comment'></div>吾君永保南山寿。车骑往来千万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364923_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1364923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　在洛。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d223908dd95f4b579c7b1c3ec8261717_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=687&endYear=687')">687年</a>　友人赵贞固离洛，赋诗送别。作品：送赵六贞固。<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵贞固，名元（一作元亮），自号昭夷子，汲人，年二十七游洛阳，授豳州宜禄县尉，与道士司马子微及卢藏用、魏元忠、陆庆余、王适、宋之问、陈子昂等友善，万岁登封元年（六九六）卒于汴州，年三十九。见陈子昂《昭夷子赵氏碣颂》。《新唐书·赵元传》：“来游洛阳，士争向慕……武后方称制，惧不容其高，调宜禄尉。”赵元于中宗嗣圣元年（六八四）年二十七，来游洛阳，正值武后初临朝称制时，诗当此年后、万岁登封元年前作。姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_22248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赵六贞固</a><span class='authorDate'>（687年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22248")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22248", 22248, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>心醉</span>东郊柳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22248'>怨别此何时，春<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作青）</span>芳来已久。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22248'>与君共时物，尽此盈樽酒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22248'>始愿今不从，春风恋携手。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22248'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22248_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=691')">689-691年</a>，34-36岁</div><div id='115eb4c2ab694bd2bb95b17eb3674e62' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　居洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年春</a>　为习艺馆学士，与杨炯分直于洛城西。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　与杨炯同为习艺馆学士，供职宫中，作双鹤诗自喻。作品：题九州院双鹤。<span class='inlineComment2'>（杨炯（650-约693）华阴人，官至盈川令。著文集三十卷，与王勃、卢照邻、骆宾王合称“四杰”，《旧唐书》卷一九○上、《新唐书》卷二○一有传。）</span><div id='poem_22171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题九州院双鹤</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22171")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22171'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22171'>君门九重闭，中有天泉池。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22171'>可怜双白鹤，飞下碧松枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22171'>吹楼多清管，鸣舞共差池。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22171'>常欲万里去，怀恩终在斯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22171'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年秋</a>　与杨炯同为习艺馆学士，供职宫中，赋馆中秋莲。作品：秋莲赋并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（杨炯（650-约693）华阴人，官至盈川令。著文集三十卷，与王勃、卢照邻、骆宾王合称“四杰”，《旧唐书》卷一九○上、《新唐书》卷二○一有传。）</span><div id='poem_1364924' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364924' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364924?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋莲赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364924")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364924_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364924'>天授元年。敕学士杨炯与之问分直于洛城西入閤。每鸡鸣后。至羽林仗。阍人奏名请龟契。伫命拱立于御桥之西。玉池清泠。红蕖菡萏。谬履扃闼。自春徂秋。见其生。视其长。睹其盛。惜其衰。得终天年而无夭折者。良以隔碍仙禁。人莫由窥。向若生于潇湘洞庭。溱洧淇澳。即有吴姬越客。郑女卫童。芳心未成。采撷都尽。今委以白露。顺以凉风。荣落有期。私分毕矣。斐然愿歌其事。久之乃述秋莲赋焉。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364924_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364924'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364924'>若夫西城秘掖。北禁仙流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364924_comment'></div>见白露之先降。悲红蕖之巳秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364924_comment'></div>昔之菡萏齐秀。芬敷竞发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364924_comment'></div>君门閟兮九重。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364924", 1364924, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>兵卫</span>俨兮千列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364924_comment'></div>绿叶青枝。缘沟覆池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364924_comment'></div>映连旗以摇艳。辉长剑兮陆离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364924_comment'></div>疏瀍兮裂谷。交流兮相沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364924_comment'></div>四绕兮丹禁。三匝兮承明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364924_comment'></div>晓而望之。若霓裳宛转朝玉京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364924_comment'></div>夕而察之。若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364924", 1364924, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>霞标</span>灼烁散赤城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364924_comment'></div>既如秦女艳日兮凤鸣。又如洛妃拾翠兮鸿惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364924_comment'></div>足使瑶草罢色。芳树无情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364924_comment'></div>复道兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364924", 1364924, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>诘曲</span>。离宫兮相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364924_comment'></div>飞阁兮周庐。金铺兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364924", 1364924, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>璧除</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364924_comment'></div>君之驾兮旖旎。莲之叶兮扶疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364924_comment'></div>万乘顾兮驻䌽骑。六宫喜兮停罗裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364924_comment'></div>仰仙游而德泽。纵元览而神虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364924_comment'></div>岂与夫溪涧兮沼沚。自生兮自死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364924_comment'></div>海圻兮江沱。万里兮烟波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364924_comment'></div>泛汉女。游湘娥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364924_comment'></div>佩鸣玉。戏清涡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364924_comment'></div>中流欲渡兮木兰楫。幽泉一曲兮采莲歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364924_comment'></div>江南兮岘北。汀洲兮不极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364924_comment'></div>既有芳兮莎城。长无依兮水国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364924_comment'></div>岂知移植天泉。飘香列仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364924_comment'></div>娇紫台之月露。含玉宇之风烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364924_comment'></div>杂葩兮照烛。众彩兮相宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364924_comment'></div>鸟翡翠兮舟青翰。树珊瑚兮林碧鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364924_comment'></div>夫其生也。春风昼荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364924_comment'></div>烁日相煎。夭桃尽兮秾李灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364924_comment'></div>出大堤兮艳欲然。夫其谢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364924_comment'></div>秋灰度琯。金气腾天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364924_comment'></div>宫槐疏兮井桐变。摇寒波兮风飒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364924_comment'></div>归根息艳兮八九月。乘化无穷兮千万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364924_comment'></div>越人望兮长巳矣。郑女采兮无由缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364924_comment'></div>何深蒂之能固。何秾香之独全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364924_comment'></div>别有待制扬雄。悲秋宋玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364924_comment'></div>夏之来兮玩早红。秋之暮兮悲馀绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364924_comment'></div>礼盛燕台。人非楚材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364924_comment'></div>云雾图兮兰为阁。金银酒兮莲作杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364924_comment'></div>落英兮俳徊。风转兮衰颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364924_comment'></div>入黄扉兮洒锦石。萦白蘋兮覆绿苔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364924_comment'></div>寒暑茫茫兮代谢。故叶新花兮往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364924_comment'></div>何秋日之可哀。托芙蓉以为媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364924_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1364924_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年冬</a>　杨炯卒盈川任，其弟扶榇归葬，经洛阳，宋作文哭祭。作品：祭杨盈川文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陶注仅云杨炯约卒于本年，未系祭文年月。按：文中有“帷席何依，冰雪四满”，杨炯归榇经洛或在本年冬。宋之问本年秋尚在京兆蓝田，或冬已返洛。）</span><div id='poem_1364951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1364951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364951'>维大周某年月日。西河宋某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364951_comment'></div>谨以清酌脯羞之奠。敬祭于杨子之灵曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364951_comment'></div>自古皆死。不朽者文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364951_comment'></div>北河流液。西岳吐云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364951_comment'></div>叶神通契。降精于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364951_comment'></div>伏道孔门。游刃诸子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364951_comment'></div>精微博识。黄中通理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364951_comment'></div>属词比事。宗经匠史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364951_comment'></div>玉璞金浑。风摇云起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364951_comment'></div>闻人之善。若在诸已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364951_comment'></div>受人之恩。许之以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364951_comment'></div>惟子坚刚。气陵秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364951_comment'></div>行不苟合。言不苟忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364951_comment'></div>大君有命。徵子文房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364951_comment'></div>余亦叨忝。随君颉颃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364951_comment'></div>同趋北禁。并拜东堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364951_comment'></div>志事俱得。形骸两忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364951_comment'></div>载罹寒暑。贫病洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364951_comment'></div>裘马同弊。老幼均粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364951_comment'></div>自君出宰。南浮江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364951_comment'></div>余尝苦饥。今日犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364951_comment'></div>之子妙年。香名早传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364951_comment'></div>从来金马。夙昔崇贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364951_comment'></div>门庭若市。翰墨如泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364951_comment'></div>千载之后。闻而凛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364951_comment'></div>死而不亡。问余何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364951_comment'></div>伤予命薄。益友零落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364951_comment'></div>生平之言。幽显相托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364951_comment'></div>痛君不嗣。匪我孤诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364951_comment'></div>君有兄弟。同心异体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364951_comment'></div>陟冈增哀。归葬以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364951_comment'></div>旅榇飘零。于洛之汀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364951_comment'></div>我之怀矣。感叹入冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364951_comment'></div>见子之弟。类子之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364951_comment'></div>悼往心绝。慰存涕盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364951_comment'></div>古人有言。一死一生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364951_comment'></div>昔子往矣。追送倾城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364951_comment'></div>今子来也。乃知交情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364951_comment'></div>惟郭是戚。有崔不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364951_comment'></div>来哭来祭。哀文在席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364951_comment'></div>帷席可依。冰雪四满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364951_comment'></div>家人哀哀。宾径微断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364951_comment'></div>今我伤悲。情勤昔时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364951_comment'></div>子文子翰。我缄我持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364951_comment'></div>子宅子兆。我营我思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364951_comment'></div>子有神鉴。我言不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364951_comment'></div>我有絮酒。子其歆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364951_comment'></div>我亦引满。傥昭神期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364951_comment'></div>魂兮归来。闻余此词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364951_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1364951_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=695&endYear=695')">695年</a>　在洛阳为官，且预宫中游宴，或已任洛州参军。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8f281724695f432cb8e60af9db0cb797_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=695&endYear=695')">695年7月</a>　上阳宫宴群臣，则天赋诗，群臣奉和，命宋编纪众作，为序。作品：早秋上阳宫侍宴序。<div id='poem_1364936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>早秋上阳宫侍宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_1364936")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364936'>臣闻神器至大。非圣无以光临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364936_comment'></div>宝位至尊。非神无以长守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364936_comment'></div>我金轮圣神皇帝垂妙觉。抚鸿勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364936_comment'></div>出轩宫而镇紫微。卷翚衣而袭元兖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364936_comment'></div>释罘祝网。万族咸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364936_comment'></div>革故维新。五刑不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364936_comment'></div>润玉律而含元气。转金浑而调顺晷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364936_comment'></div>穷荒极远。重译左言之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364936_comment'></div>负阻凭危。背德殊风之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364936_comment'></div>莫不厥角稽颡。执贽来庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364936_comment'></div>烟火通于万方。车书混于千界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364936_comment'></div>庆延八室。享配于明祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364936_comment'></div>辟水三雍。讲论乎道义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364936_comment'></div>麟凤荐祉。龟龙奉图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364936_comment'></div>石铭显瑞于郊畿。玉书告祥于宫掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364936_comment'></div>以日继月。纷纶葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364936_comment'></div>竹帛书之而未穷。夷夏歌之而不极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364936_comment'></div>圣人之具品周矣。天子之能事毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364936_comment'></div>自千古以下。迄于梁隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364936_comment'></div>何功于人。比我全德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364936_comment'></div>于是宁宴坐。展豫游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364936_comment'></div>顺四时。乘六辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364936_comment'></div>先王洛食。上帝河都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364936_comment'></div>枢机正于域中。雨露均于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364936_comment'></div>徒观其离宫别殿。弥复道而亘南端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364936_comment'></div>高阁重甍。瞰崇墉而连北斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364936_comment'></div>沧洲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364936", 1364936, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>晓气</span>。化为宫阙之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364936_comment'></div>阊阖秋风。乱起金银之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364936_comment'></div>降雕舆而式燕。簪绋凝严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364936_comment'></div>披镂槛而升高。山河在目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364936_comment'></div>参光有地。游日月于天边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364936_comment'></div>睨远无穷。见城池于掌上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364936_comment'></div>四达分九重之路。积树捎云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364936_comment'></div>双茎当铁锁之桥。流珠耿汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364936_comment'></div>霞浆玉醴。与湛露而俱倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364936_comment'></div>凤管<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364936", 1364936, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>龙丝</span>。杂商飙而共奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364936_comment'></div>圣皇乃望芝田。赋葛天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364936_comment'></div>和者万。唱者千。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年春</a>　龙门应制，与东方虬争胜。作品：龙门应制。<span /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　卧病闻杜审言贬吉州，赋诗以送。作品：送杜审言。<span class='inlineComment2'>（杜审言：字必简，祖籍襄阳，迁居巩县。咸亨元年登进士第，授隰城尉，累转洛阳丞。圣历元年，贬吉州司户参军，被构下狱，免官还洛阳。授著作郎，俄迁膳部员外郎。神龙元年，因阿附张易之，流峰州。二年召还，授国子监主簿，加修文馆直学士。景龙二年卒，年六十余。少与李峤、崔融、苏味道齐名，号文章四友。有文集十卷。《旧唐书》卷一九○上、《新唐书》卷二○一有传。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第255页杜审言条。）</span><div class='inlineComment2'>（司马承祯，字子微，少好学，薄于为吏，遂为道士，师嵩山潘师正，后止于天台山。曾受武后、睿宗征召入京，玄宗朝再征。居王屋山，卒，赐谥贞一先生。道教上清派尊为第十二代宗师。事迹见《旧唐书》卷一九二、《新唐书》卷一九六本传及卫凭《唐王屋山中岩台贞一先生庙碣》。参周祖撰《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第154页司马承祯条。）</span><div
