id='poem_sentence_14_22250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_22250'>主人丝管清且悲，客子肝肠断还续。<div id='poem_sentence_15_22250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_22250'>荔浦蘅皋万里馀，洛阳音信绝能疏。<div id='poem_sentence_16_22250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_22250'>故园今日应愁思，曲水何能更祓除。<div id='poem_sentence_17_22250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_22250'>逐伴谁怜合浦叶，思归岂食桂江鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_18_22250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_22250'>不求汉使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_22250", 22250, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>金囊</span>赠，愿得佳人锦字书。<div id='poem_sentence_19_22250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_22250'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_22250_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年春</a>　流寓桂州，过蛮峒，有诗。作品：过蛮峒。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陶注仅云诗当景云中贬钦州后作。按：诗云“园香覆橘花。”橘花期在春季，诗当春日作，景云元年六月之问自越流钦，二年春尚在途中，味诗意不似流途中之悲苦，故此诗盖先天元年流寓桂州时作。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年秋</a>　流寓桂州，秋日有诗抒怀。作品：始安秋日。<div id='poem_22196' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22196' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
昭平（龙平）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f383dbf5fa5544d3a4c2424370a8571e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f383dbf5fa5544d3a4c2424370a8571e");'><span id='f383dbf5fa5544d3a4c2424370a8571e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年</a>，57岁</div><div id='f383dbf5fa5544d3a4c2424370a8571e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>自桂州赴梧州，经桂江悬黎壁，有诗。作品：下桂江县黎壁。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陶注云：“县黎壁：当是江岸畔石壁，以石质晶莹如县黎（美玉）得名。”未言地在桂江何处。据金石声《校正宋之问〈下桂江县黎壁〉》(《学术论坛》1982年01期)考，县黎壁即今昭平县之上下悬藤滩、雷劈滩，今从。按，《广西通志》卷一一三云：“平乐江中有悬藤滩黎壁滩”，《太平寰宇记》卷一六三昭州平乐县：“平乐江在县东八十里，江中有悬藤滩、犁壁湍。”平乐江为桂江支流，宋之问下桂江赴梧州不经此处。则桂江，平乐江中均有悬藤滩，黎壁滩（或湍），盖悬藤、黎壁之名，为当地江势险要类似之处之通称。此诗《文苑英华》卷三一七、《全唐诗》卷一六○重收作孟浩然诗，然宋刻蜀本《孟浩然诗集》不载。且《诗式》卷四、《又玄集》卷上、《文苑英华》卷二九○及《永乐大典、《诗渊》等均收为宋之问诗，孟浩然生平无贬岭南之经历，诗为宋之问作无疑。）</span><div id='poem_22214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>下桂江县黎壁</a><span class='authorDate'>（712年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22214")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22214'>放溜觌前溆，连山分<span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22214", 22214, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>江回</span>云壁转，天小雾峰攒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22214'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_22214", 22214, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>吼沫</span>跳急浪，合流环峻滩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22214'>欹离<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作杂）</span>出漩划，缭绕避<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22214", 22214, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>涡盘</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22214'>舟子怯桂水，最言斯路难。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22214'>吾生抱忠信，吟啸自安闲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22214'>企予见夜月，委曲破林峦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22214'>潭旷竹烟尽，洲香橘露团。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22214'>岂傲夙所好，对之与俱欢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>自桂州赴梧州，经桂江龙目滩，有诗。作品：下桂江龙目滩。<span -----title
梧州（苍梧）
-----detail

-----title
广州（南海）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c38b1e0f1d8c43be928b62c32ac18cd9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c38b1e0f1d8c43be928b62c32ac18cd9");'><span id='c38b1e0f1d8c43be928b62c32ac18cd9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年</a>，57岁</div><div id='c38b1e0f1d8c43be928b62c32ac18cd9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>先天元年，宋沿桂江南下经梧州，复沿西江赴广州，投广州长史朱齐之，陪观妓，有诗。作品：广州朱长史宅观妓。<span class='inlineComment2'>（朱长史：朱齐之，字思贤，吴郡人，历宋州虞城尉、广州录事参军、左台监察御史、湖州武源令，桂州司马、广州都督府长史，开元二年六月卒于广州官舍，年六十二。见《唐代墓志汇编·唐故通议大夫行广州都督府长史上柱国朱府君墓志铭并序》。此诗似为残篇。）</span><div id='poem_22074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广州朱长史座观妓</a><span class='authorDate'>（712年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22074")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_22074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22074'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22074'>歌舞须<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22074", 22074, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>连夜</span>，神仙莫放归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22074'>参差随暮雨，前路湿人衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22074'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_22074_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在广州，登越王台揽胜及北望乡关，有诗。作品：登粤王台。<div id='poem_22210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登粤王台</a><span class='authorDate'>（712年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13975, "初唐", "宋之问", "poem_title_22210")'>宋之问</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22210_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22210'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4572, "poem_allusion_22210")'>贾谊</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22210'>江上粤王台，登高望几回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22210'>南溟天外合，北户日边开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22210'>地湿烟尝起，山晴雨半来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22210'>冬花采卢橘，夏果摘杨梅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22210'>迹类虞翻枉，人非<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4572, "poem_sentence_4_22210")'>贾谊</span>才。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22210'>归心不可见<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作度）</span>，白发重相催。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22210'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22210_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

清远

id='poem_content_22179'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22179'>传闻峡山好，旭日棹前沂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22179", 22179, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>雨色</span>摇丹嶂，泉声聒翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22179'>两岩天作带，万壑树披衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22179'>秋菊迎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22179", 22179, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>霜序</span>，春藤碍日辉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22179'>翳潭花似织，缘岭竹成围。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22179'>寂历环<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_22179", 22179, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>沙浦</span>，葱茏转石圻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22179'>露馀江未热，风落瘴初稀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_22179", 22179, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>猿饮</span>排虚上，禽惊掠水飞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_22179", 22179, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>榜童</span>夷唱合，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_22179", 22179, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>樵女</span>越吟归。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22179'>良候斯为美，边愁自有违。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22179'>谁言望乡国，流涕失芳菲。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22179'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_22179_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在广州，游北江中宿峡，宿广庆寺，有诗。作品：宿峡山寺。<div id='poem_22151' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22151' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22151?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_22151'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22151", 22151, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>香岫</span>悬金刹，飞泉届<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作界）</span>石门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22151'>空山唯习静，中夜寂无喧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22151'>说法初闻鸟，看心欲定猿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22151'>寥寥隔尘市<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作事）</span>，何异<span
